Decrypted data is accessible by any application installed on device.\r\n\r\nApplication provides two methods to encrypt and decrypt data.  Each method has advantages and disadvantages.  Choose which method to use depending on data size and intended use.\r\n\r\nFirst method places folder or file into an archive file and then encrypts archive file.  Files in folder cannot be seen since they were placed into one file.  Sharing content is simple since only one file needs to be exchanged. This method will exceed device memory limits more often than second method since encrypting one large file versus many smaller files.  This method is always slower than second method.\r\n\r\nSecond method encrypts individual files located in hierarchy of AES folder.
